https://lowcostlasers.com/product/hand-sanitizer-covid-19/#tab-description   Trinity Astanza laser machine ? LowCostLasers
Description
Trinity Astanza laser machine.
Q-switched Nd:YAG laser
1064 nm wavelength w/ fluence up to 28 J/cm2 @ 2 mm
532 nm wavelength w/ fluence up to 14 J/cm2 @ 2 mm
6 ns pulse duration
Up to 10 Hz repetition rate
Touchscreen interface
"Electrical requirements: 220-230 V AC, 50/60 Hz, 16 A"
Astanza Laser?s Trinity laser offers tattoo removal practitioners the opportunity to provide all-color
removal of tattoos with a combination Nd:YAG and Ruby laser. The innovative inclusion of a q-
switched Ruby laser (694nm) with a q-switched Nd:YAG laser (1064nm and 532nm) allows for the
"creation of a powerful three wavelength system. Highly effective at removing black, purple, brown, red,"
"orange, and yellow tattoos, Nd:YAG lasers are the traditional systems for tattoo removal"

The Sciton JOULE Multi-Application Laser treats:
Uneven skin tone
Acne and acne scars
Fine lines and wrinkles
Scars
Brown spots
Skin laxity
Unwanted hair
Sciton JOULE Treatments:
Micro Laser Peel
Deep skin peeling for wrinkle reduction
Fractional laser skin resurfacing
Removal of sun and age spots
Reduction of acne scars and acne management
Skin firming
Laser hair removal
Vascular treatment
Smart Filters and different wavelengths:
420 ? Acne
"515 ? Pigmented Lesions, such as freckles, age spots."
"560 ? Vascular Lesions, such as cherry angiomas, telangiectasias, and rosacea."
590 ? Deeper Lesions / Darker Skin Types
"590, 640 & 695 ? Hair Removal"
The Sciton JOULE system is?appropriately enough?the crown jewel of Sciton?s currently available
"products. An update to Sciton?s popular Sciton Profile series of products, the JOULE has the capacity"
to carry out more cosmetic medical procedures than practically any system in existence. The JOULE
"can deliver treatments across a number of energy wavelengths via laser light, infrared, ultrasound, and"
"applied heat. Using OptiPlex technology, the JOULE allows practitioners to design their own treatment"
"regimens, and can deliver laser pulses at a number of different wavelengths of light as desired: at a"
"single wavelength, blended together, or multiplexed into a series of alternating wavelengths."
The JOULE platform is designed so that practitioners can expand their practices by acquiring new
"modules as desired. This has proven to be an incredibly popular and convenient system, minimizing"
customer costs while maximizing options. Some of the most popular JOULE modules include:
Sciton JOULE BBL
Sciton?s BBL (BroadBand Light) module uses technology for treatments commonly referred to as IPL
"(Intense Pulsed Light) or photo-facials. The BBL handpiece uses a dual-lamp system, which greatly"
"extends the lifespan of the unit. The handpiece applicator is placed against targeted areas of the skin,"
and projects highly energetic pulses of broad spectrum light into the skin and subdermal tissue. At the
"same time, an integrating cooling system monitors the temperature of the exposed tissue, and"
"maintains a comfortable temperature, which can be set by the user to anywhere between 0 and 30"
"degrees Celsius, as desired."
Treatment options are determined by the use of interchangeable filters and adapters that adapt the
light wavelength and spot size and shape of the projection spot. Multiple skin conditions can be treated
"in a single session simply by changing out the included Smart Filters, and Finesse adapters can be"
attached to the handpiece to more effectively treat different areas of the body.
The Sciton BBL system is currently indicated for clinical treatments including:
"Treatment of acne, including cases that manifests as inflammatory lesions, nodules, and cysts"
"Reducing the visibility of small pigmented lesions, such as freckles and those resulting from sun"
damage
"Removing angiomas, spider veins, and other vascular lesions"
"Reducing generalized skin redness, such as that caused by rosacea"
Treating larger pigmented lesions such as port-wine stains and cafe-au-laits
Permanently reducing and removing unwanted facial and body hair

https://lowcostlasers.com/product/hand-sanitizer-covid-19/?add-to-cart=1449   Trinity Astanza laser machine ? LowCostLasers
Description
Trinity Astanza laser machine.
Q-switched Nd:YAG laser
1064 nm wavelength w/ fluence up to 28 J/cm2 @ 2 mm
532 nm wavelength w/ fluence up to 14 J/cm2 @ 2 mm
6 ns pulse duration
Up to 10 Hz repetition rate
Touchscreen interface
"Electrical requirements: 220-230 V AC, 50/60 Hz, 16 A"
Astanza Laser?s Trinity laser offers tattoo removal practitioners the opportunity to provide all-color
removal of tattoos with a combination Nd:YAG and Ruby laser. The innovative inclusion of a q-
switched Ruby laser (694nm) with a q-switched Nd:YAG laser (1064nm and 532nm) allows for the
"creation of a powerful three wavelength system. Highly effective at removing black, purple, brown, red,"
"orange, and yellow tattoos, Nd:YAG lasers are the traditional systems for tattoo removal"

Trinity Astanza laser machine.
Q-switched Nd:YAG laser
1064 nm wavelength w/ fluence up to 28 J/cm2 @ 2 mm
532 nm wavelength w/ fluence up to 14 J/cm2 @ 2 mm
6 ns pulse duration
Up to 10 Hz repetition rate
Touchscreen interface

Astanza Laser?s Trinity laser offers tattoo removal practitioners the opportunity to provide all-color

"creation of a powerful three wavelength system. Highly effective at removing black, purple, brown, red,"

https://lowcostlasers.com/product/trinity-astanza-laser-machine/?add-to-      Trinity Astanza laser machine ? LowCostLasers
cart=1964                                                                     Description
Trinity Astanza laser machine.
Q-switched Nd:YAG laser
1064 nm wavelength w/ fluence up to 28 J/cm2 @ 2 mm
532 nm wavelength w/ fluence up to 14 J/cm2 @ 2 mm
6 ns pulse duration
Up to 10 Hz repetition rate
Touchscreen interface
"Electrical requirements: 220-230 V AC, 50/60 Hz, 16 A"
Astanza Laser?s Trinity laser offers tattoo removal practitioners the opportunity to provide all-color
removal of tattoos with a combination Nd:YAG and Ruby laser. The innovative inclusion of a q-
switched Ruby laser (694nm) with a q-switched Nd:YAG laser (1064nm and 532nm) allows for the
"creation of a powerful three wavelength system. Highly effective at removing black, purple, brown, red,"
"orange, and yellow tattoos, Nd:YAG lasers are the traditional systems for tattoo removal"

The Lumenis M22 is one of the most versatile multi-application platforms available from the Lumenis
"line of cosmetic and aesthetic medicine lasers. In fact, the multi-platform can treat over 30 skin"
conditions while still providing industry-leading laser hair removal.
"The Lumenis M22 includes four technologies in one modular system, designed to help your practice"
grow and adapt to future applications as they emerge. These four technologies include:
Universal Intense Pulsed Light (IPL)
Optimal pulse technology for photorejuvenation
Single handpiece with changeable filters and lightguides
Multi-Spot Nd:YAG
Multiple Sequential Pulsing (MSP)
Ideal for treating leg veins and vascular lesions
Q-switched Nd:YAG
Homogenous beam profile for optimal safety and efficacy
"Ideal for treating pigmented lesions, dark tattoo removal, and other combination treatments"
"The modular capabilities of the M22 laser allow add-as-you-need treatment expansions, and with"
"streamlined simplicity, this system?s laser operation is simple from start-up through actual use. As a"
"tabletop device, the M22 is also quite portable, allowing you to move this system from exam room to"
exam room with relative ease.

Syneron Candela Profound RF Microneedle and skin tightening device. It comes with both hand
pieces and a box of tips
Syneron Candela?s Profound system is the only fractional RF microneedle system authorized to be
sold in the United States under the MGH patents. Invented and developed by leaders in aesthetic
"dermatology, the Profound system offers a minimally-invasive procedure clinically proven to treat facial"
wrinkles and cellulite with a single treatment. The Profound treatment stimulates the body?s natural
"production of elastin, collagen and hyaluronic acid, resulting in the creation of three important building"
blocks for youthful looking skin. Profound has FDA clearance for use in the treatment of both the face
and body.
Profound Microneedle RF technology offers remarkable advantages. Patients can enjoy the dramatic
results of a mini-facelift in the most natural yet least invasive way possible. It is a non-surgical
"procedure that allows for minimal downtime, with most patients returning to normal activities within 24"
to 48 hours. Profound Microneedle RF technology is ideal for patients who want a natural approach in
"facial rejuvenation, as it does not rely on fillers or injectables. Instead, dermal volume and elasticity are"
formed by triggering the body?s own natural healing process within the deep dermis layer of the skin

https://lowcostlasers.com/product/trinity-astanza-laser-machine/?add-to-      Trinity Astanza laser machine ? LowCostLasers
cart=1969                                                                     Description
Trinity Astanza laser machine.
Q-switched Nd:YAG laser
1064 nm wavelength w/ fluence up to 28 J/cm2 @ 2 mm
532 nm wavelength w/ fluence up to 14 J/cm2 @ 2 mm
6 ns pulse duration
Up to 10 Hz repetition rate
Touchscreen interface
"Electrical requirements: 220-230 V AC, 50/60 Hz, 16 A"
Astanza Laser?s Trinity laser offers tattoo removal practitioners the opportunity to provide all-color
removal of tattoos with a combination Nd:YAG and Ruby laser. The innovative inclusion of a q-
switched Ruby laser (694nm) with a q-switched Nd:YAG laser (1064nm and 532nm) allows for the
"creation of a powerful three wavelength system. Highly effective at removing black, purple, brown, red,"
"orange, and yellow tattoos, Nd:YAG lasers are the traditional systems for tattoo removal"

The Sciton JOULE Multi-Application Laser treats:
Uneven skin tone
Acne and acne scars
Fine lines and wrinkles
Scars
Brown spots
Skin laxity
Unwanted hair
Sciton JOULE Treatments:
Micro Laser Peel
Deep skin peeling for wrinkle reduction
Fractional laser skin resurfacing
Removal of sun and age spots
Reduction of acne scars and acne management
Skin firming
Laser hair removal
Vascular treatment
Smart Filters and different wavelengths:
420 ? Acne
"515 ? Pigmented Lesions, such as freckles, age spots."
"560 ? Vascular Lesions, such as cherry angiomas, telangiectasias, and rosacea."
590 ? Deeper Lesions / Darker Skin Types
"590, 640 & 695 ? Hair Removal"
The Sciton JOULE system is?appropriately enough?the crown jewel of Sciton?s currently available
"products. An update to Sciton?s popular Sciton Profile series of products, the JOULE has the capacity"
to carry out more cosmetic medical procedures than practically any system in existence. The JOULE
"can deliver treatments across a number of energy wavelengths via laser light, infrared, ultrasound, and"
"applied heat. Using OptiPlex technology, the JOULE allows practitioners to design their own treatment"
"regimens, and can deliver laser pulses at a number of different wavelengths of light as desired: at a"
"single wavelength, blended together, or multiplexed into a series of alternating wavelengths."
The JOULE platform is designed so that practitioners can expand their practices by acquiring new
"modules as desired. This has proven to be an incredibly popular and convenient system, minimizing"
customer costs while maximizing options. Some of the most popular JOULE modules include:
Sciton JOULE BBL
Sciton?s BBL (BroadBand Light) module uses technology for treatments commonly referred to as IPL
"(Intense Pulsed Light) or photo-facials. The BBL handpiece uses a dual-lamp system, which greatly"
"extends the lifespan of the unit. The handpiece applicator is placed against targeted areas of the skin,"
and projects highly energetic pulses of broad spectrum light into the skin and subdermal tissue. At the
"same time, an integrating cooling system monitors the temperature of the exposed tissue, and"
"maintains a comfortable temperature, which can be set by the user to anywhere between 0 and 30"
"degrees Celsius, as desired."
Treatment options are determined by the use of interchangeable filters and adapters that adapt the
light wavelength and spot size and shape of the projection spot. Multiple skin conditions can be treated
"in a single session simply by changing out the included Smart Filters, and Finesse adapters can be"
attached to the handpiece to more effectively treat different areas of the body.
The Sciton BBL system is currently indicated for clinical treatments including:
"Treatment of acne, including cases that manifests as inflammatory lesions, nodules, and cysts"
"Reducing the visibility of small pigmented lesions, such as freckles and those resulting from sun"
damage
"Removing angiomas, spider veins, and other vascular lesions"
"Reducing generalized skin redness, such as that caused by rosacea"
Treating larger pigmented lesions such as port-wine stains and cafe-au-laits
Permanently reducing and removing unwanted facial and body hair

"products. An update to Sciton?s popular Sciton Profile series of products, the JOULE has the capacity"
to carry out more cosmetic medical procedures than practically any system in existence. The JOULE
"can deliver treatments across a number of energy wavelengths via laser light, infrared, ultrasound, and"
"applied heat. Using OptiPlex technology, the JOULE allows practitioners to design their own treatment"
"regimens, and can deliver laser pulses at a number of different wavelengths of light as desired: at a"
"single wavelength, blended together, or multiplexed into a series of alternating wavelengths."
The JOULE platform is designed so that practitioners can expand their practices by acquiring new
"modules as desired. This has proven to be an incredibly popular and convenient system, minimizing"
customer costs while maximizing options. Some of the most popular JOULE modules include:
Sciton JOULE BBL
Sciton?s BBL (BroadBand Light) module uses technology for treatments commonly referred to as IPL
"(Intense Pulsed Light) or photo-facials. The BBL handpiece uses a dual-lamp system, which greatly"
"extends the lifespan of the unit. The handpiece applicator is placed against targeted areas of the skin,"
and projects highly energetic pulses of broad spectrum light into the skin and subdermal tissue. At the
"same time, an integrating cooling system monitors the temperature of the exposed tissue, and"
"maintains a comfortable temperature, which can be set by the user to anywhere between 0 and 30"
"degrees Celsius, as desired."
Treatment options are determined by the use of interchangeable filters and adapters that adapt the
light wavelength and spot size and shape of the projection spot. Multiple skin conditions can be treated
"in a single session simply by changing out the included Smart Filters, and Finesse adapters can be"
attached to the handpiece to more effectively treat different areas of the body.
The Sciton BBL system is currently indicated for clinical treatments including:
"Treatment of acne, including cases that manifests as inflammatory lesions, nodules, and cysts"
"Reducing the visibility of small pigmented lesions, such as freckles and those resulting from sun"
damage
"Removing angiomas, spider veins, and other vascular lesions"
"Reducing generalized skin redness, such as that caused by rosacea"
Treating larger pigmented lesions such as port-wine stains and cafe-au-laits
Permanently reducing and removing unwanted facial and body hair

420 ? Acne
"515 ? Pigmented Lesions, such as freckles, age spots."

590 ? Deeper Lesions / Darker Skin Types

The Sciton JOULE system is?appropriately enough?the crown jewel of Sciton?s currently available
"products. An update to Sciton?s popular Sciton Profile series of products, the JOULE has the capacity"
to carry out more cosmetic medical procedures than practically any system in existence. The JOULE
"can deliver treatments across a number of energy wavelengths via laser light, infrared, ultrasound, and"
"applied heat. Using OptiPlex technology, the JOULE allows practitioners to design their own treatment"
"regimens, and can deliver laser pulses at a number of different wavelengths of light as desired: at a"
"single wavelength, blended together, or multiplexed into a series of alternating wavelengths."
The JOULE platform is designed so that practitioners can expand their practices by acquiring new
"modules as desired. This has proven to be an incredibly popular and convenient system, minimizing"
customer costs while maximizing options. Some of the most popular JOULE modules include:
Sciton JOULE BBL
Sciton?s BBL (BroadBand Light) module uses technology for treatments commonly referred to as IPL
"(Intense Pulsed Light) or photo-facials. The BBL handpiece uses a dual-lamp system, which greatly"
"extends the lifespan of the unit. The handpiece applicator is placed against targeted areas of the skin,"
and projects highly energetic pulses of broad spectrum light into the skin and subdermal tissue. At the
"same time, an integrating cooling system monitors the temperature of the exposed tissue, and"
"maintains a comfortable temperature, which can be set by the user to anywhere between 0 and 30"
"degrees Celsius, as desired."
Treatment options are determined by the use of interchangeable filters and adapters that adapt the
light wavelength and spot size and shape of the projection spot. Multiple skin conditions can be treated
"in a single session simply by changing out the included Smart Filters, and Finesse adapters can be"
attached to the handpiece to more effectively treat different areas of the body.
The Sciton BBL system is currently indicated for clinical treatments including:
"Treatment of acne, including cases that manifests as inflammatory lesions, nodules, and cysts"
"Reducing the visibility of small pigmented lesions, such as freckles and those resulting from sun"
damage
"Removing angiomas, spider veins, and other vascular lesions"
"Reducing generalized skin redness, such as that caused by rosacea"
Treating larger pigmented lesions such as port-wine stains and cafe-au-laits
Permanently reducing and removing unwanted facial and body hair

"picosecond laser designed for multiple aesthetic applications, the PicoSure is the only aesthetic laser"
that can magnify pressure up to 70% and widths up to 550pps.

Picosecond technology with a unique Focus Lens Array for the most effective skin revitalization
"results. A remarkable tool for use in wrinkle reduction, removal of tough acne scars, tattoo removal and"
